   CLAIMS
   1. A mutant v3 or v2 fHbp which is:
      (A) a polypeptide comprising a mutant fHbp v2 amino acid sequence, wherein: (a) the amino
          acid sequence has at least 80% sequence identity to SEQ ID NO: 5 and/or comprises a
 5        fragment of SEQ ID NO: 5 which is at least 7 amino acids long and contains S32 from SEQ
          ID NO: 5; but (b) the amino acid sequence differs from SEQ ID NO: 5 at residue S32,
          provided that if the mutant fHbp v2 amino acid sequence includes a substitution at residue 32
          alone, either this substitution is not with alanine or at least one of the following residues is
          substituted: V33, L39, L41, F69, V100, 1113, F122, L123, V124, S125, G126, L127, G128,
10        S151, H239, and/or E240;
      or
      (B) a polypeptide comprising a mutant fHbp v3 amino acid sequence, wherein: (a) the amino acid
          sequence has at least 80% sequence identity to SEQ ID NO: 17 and/or comprises a fragment
          of SEQ ID NO: 17 which is at least 7 amino acids long and contains S32 from SEQ ID NO:
15         17; but (b) the amino acid sequence differs from SEQ ID NO: 17 at residue S32, provided
          that if the mutant fHbp v3 amino acid sequence includes a substitution at residue 32 alone,
          either this substitution is not with alanine or at least one of the following residues is
          substituted: 133, L39, L41, F72, V103, T116, F125, L126, V127, S128, G129, L130, G131,
          S154, H242, and/or E243.
20 2. The polypeptide of claim 1, wherein: (A) the amino acid sequence differs from SEQ ID NO: 5 by
      substitution at S32 and one or more of V33, L39, L41, F69, V100, 1113, F122, L123, V124,
      S125, G126, L127, G128, S151, H239, and/or E240; for instance, where the substitution(s) are
      selected from the group consisting of: S32V; V33C; L39C; L41C; F69C; V100T; 1113S; F122C;
      L123R; V1241; S125G or S125T; G126D; L1271; G128A; S151C; H239R; E240H; or (B) the
25    amino acid sequence differs from SEQ ID NO: 17 by substitution at S32 and one or more of 133,
      L39, L41, F72, V103, T116, F125, L126, V127, S128, G129, L130, G131, S154, H242, and/or
      E243; for instance, where the substitution(s) are selected from the group consisting of: S32V;
      133C; L39C; L41C; F72C; V103T; T116S; F125C; L126R; V1271; S128G or S128T; G129D;
      L1301; G131A; S154C; H242R; and E243H.
30 3. The polypeptide of claim 1(A), comprising substitutions at multiple residues, wherein the
      multiple residues are selected from groups 2B, 21, 2J or 20 as follows:
          2B: residues 32 and 123;
          21: residues 32 and 125;
          2J: residues 32, 123 and 125; or
35        20: residues 32, 123, 124, 125, 126, 127 and 128.

   4. The polypeptide of claim 3, comprising substitutions S32V and L123R relative to SEQ ID NO:
      5; optionally further comprising substitutions V1241, S125G, G126D, L1271, G128A; for
      instance, comprising SEQ ID NO: 20 or SEQ ID NO: 45 or SEQ ID NO: 58.
   5. The polypeptide of claim 1(B), comprising substitutions at multiple residues, wherein the
 5    multiple residues are selected from groups 3B, 31, 3J or 30 as follows:
           3B: residues 32 and 126;
           31: residues 32 and 128;
           3J: residues 32, 126 and 128; or
           30: residues 32, 126, 127, 128, 129, 130 and 131.
10 6. The polypeptide of claim 5, comprising substitutions S32V and L126R relative to SEQ ID NO:
      17; optionally further comprising substitutions V1271, S128G, G129D, L1301, G131A; for
      instance, comprising SEQ ID NO: 44 or SEQ ID NO: 61.
   7. The polypeptide of any preceding claim, also including one or more further mutation(s) which
      disrupt(s) the polypeptide's ability to bind to human factor H; for instance, in v2 including a
15    substitution at one or more of residues R73, D203, E210, G228, S121, F122, A192, E194, V199,
      1200, L201, T213, H215, F219, T231, and E240, or in v3 including a substitution at one or more
      of residues Q35, 1178, L87, A88, V127, V202, E213, T216, H218, T234, V241, E243, and G248.
   8. A polypeptide comprising:
      *    amino acid sequence SEQ ID NO: 45, optionally with 1, 2, 3, 4, or 5 single amino acid
20         substitutions, deletions and/or insertions, wherein the polypeptide can elicit antibodies which
          bind to a meningococcal fHbp polypeptide consisting of the amino acid sequence of SEQ ID
          NO: 2 (for example, comprising amino acid sequence SEQ ID NO: 45 with 1, 2, or 3 single
           amino acid substitutions), but not mutated at residue V32 or R123;
      *    amino acid sequence SEQ ID NO: 44, optionally with 1, 2, 3, 4, or 5 single amino acid
25         substitutions, deletions and/or insertions, wherein the polypeptide can elicit antibodies which
          bind to a meningococcal fHbp polypeptide consisting of the amino acid sequence of SEQ ID
          NO: 40 (for example, comprising amino acid sequence SEQ ID NO: 44 with 1, 2, or 3 single
           amino acid substitutions), but not mutated at residue V32 or R126;
      *    amino acid sequence SEQ ID NO: 58, optionally with 1, 2, 3, 4, or 5 single amino acid
30         substitutions, deletions and/or insertions, wherein the polypeptide can elicit antibodies which
          bind to a meningococcal fHbp polypeptide consisting of the amino acid sequence of SEQ ID
          NO: 2 (for example, comprising amino acid sequence SEQ ID NO: 58 with 1, 2, or 3 single
           amino acid substitutions), but not mutated at residue V32;
      *    amino acid sequence SEQ ID NO: 61, optionally with 1, 2, 3, 4, or 5 single amino acid
35         substitutions, deletions and/or insertions, wherein the polypeptide can elicit antibodies which
          bind to a meningococcal fHbp polypeptide consisting of the amino acid sequence of SEQ ID
                                                      -54-

   WO 2015/128480                                                                 PCT/EP2015/054174
           NO: 2 (for example, comprising amino acid sequence SEQ ID NO: 61 with 1, 2, or 3 single
           amino acid substitutions), but not mutated at residue V32;
       *   a fHbp v3 amino acid sequence, wherein the v3 amino acid sequence is identical to a v3 wild
           type amino acid sequence except for a mutation at the amino acid position corresponding to
 5         Leu-126 of SEQ ID NO: 17, provided that the mutation is not a substitution to alanine
           (e.g. wherein the mutation is a substitution to arginine);
       *   a fHbp v2 amino acid sequence, wherein the v2 amino acid sequence is identical to a v2 wild
           type amino acid sequence except for a mutation at the amino acid position corresponding to
           Leu-123 of SEQ ID NO: 5, provided that the mutation is not a substitution to alanine
10         (e.g. wherein the mutation is a substitution to arginine); or
       *   amino acid sequence SEQ ID NO: 47, optionally with 1, 2, 3, 4, or 5 single amino acid
           substitutions, deletions and/or insertions, wherein the polypeptide can elicit antibodies which
           bind to each of: a meningococcal fHbp polypeptide consisting of the amino acid sequence of
           SEQ ID NO: 46; a meningococcal fHbp polypeptide consisting of the amino acid sequence of
15         SEQ ID NO: 4; and a meningococcal fHbp polypeptide consisting of the amino acid
           sequence of SEQ ID NO: 40 (for instance, consisting of SEQ ID NO: 48).
   9.  A plasmid or other nucleic acid comprising a nucleotide sequence encoding the polypeptide of
       any of claims I to 8.
   10. A host cell transformed with the plasmid of claim 9; for example, wherein the cell is a
20     meningococcal bacterium, such as a meningococcal bacterium having down-regulation or
       knockout of mItA and also optionally has down-regulation or knockout of: (i) at least one gene
       involved in rendering the lipid A portion of LPS toxic, particularly of lpxll; and/or (ii) at least
       one gene involved in the capsular polysaccharide synthesis or export, particularly of synX and/or
       ctrA..
25 11. Membrane vesicles prepared from the host cell of claim 9, wherein the vesicles include a
       polypeptide of any one of claims I to 8.
   12. An immunogenic composition comprising a polypeptide of any one of claims I to 8, or a vesicle
       of claim 11.
   13. The composition of claim 12, further comprising a second polypeptide that, when administered to
30     a mammal, elicits an antibody response that is bactericidal against meningococcus.
   14. The composition of claim 12 or claim 13, further comprising (i) a conjugated capsular saccharide
       from N.meningitidis serogroup A, C, W135 and/or Y and/or (ii) a conjugated capsular saccharide
       from S.pneumoniae
   15. A method for raising an antibody response in a mammal, comprising administering an
35     immunogenic composition of any of claims 12 to 14.
